<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*koža</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жа</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kóža</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́ж</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кожанка.html>кожанка</a> (23002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожаный.html>ко́жаный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kóžanyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожанка.html>ко́жанка</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожанка.html>кожа́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kóžanka</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kožánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожанка.html>ко́жанки</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожанка.html>кожа́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожанка.html>ко́жанки</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожанка.html>кожа́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожанка.html>ко́жанок</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожанка.html>кожа́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> type of leather jacket common during the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_Civil_War" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Russian Civil War">Russian Civil War</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кожистый.html>ко́жистый</a> (29614)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жа</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kóža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-истый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-istyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожистый.html>ко́жистый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kóžistyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>skin-like, having a skin-like surface
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кожистый.html>ко́жистый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шелк.html>шёлк</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kóžistyj</b> šólk</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">a <b>skin-like</b> (fabric of) silk</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Not to be confused with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожный.html>ко́жный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kóžnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> skin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожаный.html>ко́жаный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kóžanyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> leather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожевенный.html>коже́венный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kožévennyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">manufacturing something with leather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кожный.html>ко́жный</a> (8588)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жа</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kóža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожный.html>ко́жный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kóžnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> skin; dermal, cutaneous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кожный.html>ко́жный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ожог.html>ожо́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kóžnyj</b> ožóg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a burn <b>on the skin</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кожный.html>ко́жная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:аллергия.html>аллерги́я</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kóžnaja</b> allergíja</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>dermal</b> allergy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кожный.html>ко́жная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:проба.html>про́ба</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kóžnaja</b> próba</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>skin</b> test</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Not to be confused with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожаный.html>ко́жаный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kóžanyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> leather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожевенный.html>коже́венный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kožévennyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">manufacturing something with leather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожистый.html>ко́жистый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kóžistyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">skin-like, having a skin-like surface</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кожух.html>кожу́х</a> (10725)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kožuxъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожух.html>кожу́х</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожух.html>ко́жух</a><sup>*</sup></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kožúx</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kóžux<sup>*</sup></span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожух.html>кожуха́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожух.html>ко́жуха</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожух.html>кожухи́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожух.html>кожуха́</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожух.html>кожухо́в</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Professional usage.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li>sheepskin coat</li>
<li>casing, housing, jacket <i>of a gun</i>, paddle-box, bonnet, boot, box, cabinet, cage, case, cover, encasement, hood, mantle, sheath, shell, shroud, shrouding</li></ol>

Зализняка). <a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> просторечное <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>ти́пу</a> 3a <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударение.html>ударе́нием</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слог.html>слог</a> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:кожух.html>ко́жухи</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:кожух.html>ко́жухов</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> т. п.)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:коза.html>коза</a> (4329)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*koza</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коза.html>коза́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kozá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коза.html>козы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коза.html>ко́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коза.html>ко́з</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>goat, she-goat</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козленок.html>козлёнок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kozljónok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козленок.html>козлёнка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козленок.html>козля́та</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козленок.html>козля́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>kid, young goat</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козни.html>ко́зни</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kózni</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козни.html>ко́зней</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>intrigues, machinations

***козырек.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:козырек.html>козырёк</a> (6014)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kozyrek</i>, equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козырь.html>ко́зырь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kózyrʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ёк</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козырек.html>козырёк</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kozyrjók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козырек.html>козырька́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козырек.html>козырьки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козырек.html>козырько́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(cap) peak, visor
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:козырек.html>козырёк</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vzjatʹ pod <b>kozyrjók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to salute</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>canopy, awning</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>зы<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>рёк</b>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> trump

<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2016</b>,  <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">Троеразных</span> (lyrics), Reenboy (music),  “Street Credibility”, in  <cite><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>Во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рло</a></span></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заряжённый.html>заря́жен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:старт.html>ста́рта</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:куплет.html>купле́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> ма́нтра<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a>, ба́ртер<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рукав.html>рукаве́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:козырной.html>козырна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:карта.html>ка́рта</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пру́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> ге́тте<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спи́ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zarjážen so stárta<br />kuplét kak mántra<br />vrémja, délo, bártɛr<br />V rukavé <b>kozyrnája</b> kárta<br />Prú kak v gétte<br />V spínu nam véter</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Charged from the start<br />Strophes like mantras<br />Time, business, barter<br />In the sleeve a <b>trump</b> card<br />Balling as in the ghetto<br />In the back to us the wind</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***козырь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:козырь.html>ко́зырь</a> (13804)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Attested first from the year 1731, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kozyr</i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kozer</i>, variants of <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kozyra</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kozera</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trump; card-sharper; card-game; struggle, calamity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a dialectal variant – already attested in the 16<sup>th</sup> century in the sense “trump” – of <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kostera</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kostyra</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">card sharper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kość</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">die</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kozyrnik</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kozernik</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">card-shark; fullam-player</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<br />From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kozyrek</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">visor of the cap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> one has <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козырек.html>козырёк</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kozyrjók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<br />
Compare as another cardgame term that has passed into Russian from Polish: <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шулер.html>шу́лер</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šúler</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">card-sharp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козырь.html>ко́зырь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kózyrʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козырь.html>ко́зыря</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козырь.html>ко́зыри</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козырь.html>козыре́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>trump</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> main argument, used in the right time to gain advantage</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unrevealed or hidden advantage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припасти.html>припасённый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:козырь.html>ко́зырь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pripasjónnyj <b>kózyrʹ</b></i> ― <small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">кто́-то <a href = vnd.unilang:припас.html>припа́с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:козырь.html>ко́зырь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">któ-to pripás <b>kózyrʹ</b></i> ― <small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>high standing collar</li>
<li>canopy over a door</li>
<li>sleigh with covered back</li></ol>

***козырять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:козырять.html>козыря́ть</a> (24726)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козырь.html>ко́зырь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kózyrʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***кой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кой.html>кой</a> (462)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">кꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kъjь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">who, what, which</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">who</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-jь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*kas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">who</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">who</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кой.html>кой</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">koj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">antiquated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> how, which, who, what
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> ко́и-то <a href = vnd.unilang:веко.html>ве́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v kói-to véki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">once in a very long time</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кой.html>ко́их</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пора.html>по́р</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do kóix por?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">how long?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кой.html>ко́их</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">iz kóix</i> ― <span class="e-translation">of which; of whom</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кой.html>кой</a></b> чёрт?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>koj</b> čórt?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what the hell for?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кой.html>ко́ей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мера.html>ме́ре</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ni v kójej mére</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not in the least</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кой.html>ко́ем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>ра́зе</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ni v kójem ráze</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not on your nelly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кой.html>ко́ем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чае</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ni v kójem slúčaje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">on no account; by no means</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кой.html>ко́им</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образ.html>о́бразом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ni kóim óbrazom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is no way</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:койка.html>койка</a> (2560)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:койка.html>ко́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kójka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:койка.html>ко́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:койка.html>ко́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:койка.html>ко́ек</a></b>)

<ol><li>hammock, bunk</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кок.html>кок</a> (14975)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kok</i> ("cook")
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***кол.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кол.html>кол</a> (4161)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kolъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кол.html>кол</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kol</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кол.html>кола́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кол.html>ко́лья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кол.html>ко́льев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stake, spicket, pale</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кол.html>кол</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kol</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кол.html>кола́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кол.html>колы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колоть.html>коло́в</a></b>)
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kolben</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колба.html>ко́лба</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kólba</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колба.html>ко́лбы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колба.html>ко́лбы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колба.html>колб</a></b>)
